class="text-lg xl:text-2xl font-bold tracking-normal mb-5 text-left text-black lg:text-center md:mb-8">About TED</h4><div class="text-sm text-gray-500">TED is a nonpartisan nonprofit devoted to TED began in 1984 as a conference where Technology, Entertainment and Design converged, and today covers almost all topics  from science to business to global issues  in more than 110 languages.
